  269|       |/// For a `MacroArg` span: replace the changed portion at or after byte column `src_col`.
  270|       |///
  271|       |/// Primary strategy: exact match of `old_text` at `src_col` (works when `old_text` is
  272|       |/// already the raw argument value).
  273|       |///
  274|       |/// Fallback: find the prefix where old/new expanded text first differ, then try
  275|       |/// progressively shorter suffix lengths until we find an old fragment that actually
  276|       |/// appears in the source from `src_col`.  This handles the common case where
  277|       |/// `old_text` is the full expanded output line, not just the argument value — and
  278|       |/// avoids false suffix matches when the old string is a suffix of the new one
  279|       |/// (e.g. `literate` vs `illiterate`).
  280|      6|fn attempt_macro_arg_patch(
  281|      6|    lines: &[String],
  282|      6|    src_line: usize,
  283|      6|    src_col: u32,
  284|      6|    old_text: &str,
  285|      6|    new_text: &str,
  286|      6|) -> Option<String> {
  287|      6|    let line = lines.get(src_line)?;
                                                ^0
  288|      6|    let col = src_col as usize;
  289|       |
  290|       |    // Primary: exact col match.
  291|      6|    if col + old_text.len() <= line.len() && &line[col..col + old_text.len()] == old_text {
                                                           ^5^5   ^5   ^5
  292|      2|        let mut new_line = line.to_string();
  293|      2|        new_line.replace_range(col..col + old_text.len(), new_text);
  294|      2|        return Some(new_line);
  295|      4|    }
  296|       |
  297|       |    // Fallback.
  298|      4|    let old_chars: Vec<char> = old_text.chars().collect();
  299|      4|    let new_chars: Vec<char> = new_text.chars().collect();
  300|       |
  301|       |    // pfx: length of the common prefix between old and new.
  302|      4|    let pfx = old_chars.iter().zip(new_chars.iter())
  303|     24|        .take_while(|(a, b)| a == b).count();
                       ^4                          ^4
  304|       |
  305|       |    // max_sfx: upper bound on common suffix length.
  306|      4|    let max_sfx = old_chars.iter().rev().zip(new_chars.iter().rev())
  307|     17|        .take_while(|(a, b)| a == b).count();
                       ^4                          ^4
  308|       |
  309|      4|    let search_start = col.min(line.len());
  310|      4|    let search_region = &line[search_start..];
  311|       |
  312|       |    // Try increasing sfx values (longest fragment first) until we find an old_frag
  313|       |    // that appears in the source.  Longest-first avoids false matches on short fragments
  314|       |    // (e.g. a single "l" matching the wrong letter in the source line).

  317|      4|        if pfx >= end { continue; }

  319|      4|        if old_frag.is_empty() { continue; }
                                               ^0
  320|       |
  321|      4|        if let Some(pos) = search_region.find(old_frag.as_str()) {
                                  ^3
  322|      3|            let new_end = new_chars.len().checked_sub(sfx)?;
                                                                        ^0
  323|      3|            if pfx > new_end { continue; }
                                             ^0
  324|      3|            let new_frag: String = new_chars[pfx..new_end].iter().collect();
  325|      3|            let abs_pos = search_start + pos;
  326|      3|            let mut new_line = line.to_string();
  327|      3|            new_line.replace_range(abs_pos..abs_pos + old_frag.len(), &new_frag);
  328|      3|            return Some(new_line);
  329|      1|        }
  330|       |    }
  331|      1|    None

  334|       |/// For a `MacroBodyWithVars` span: reconstruct the body template with only the
  335|       |/// literal (non-variable) parts updated.
  336|       |///
  337|       |/// Algorithm:
  338|       |///  1. Split `body_line` into alternating literal/variable segments via `%%(...)`.
  339|       |///  2. Walk `old_expanded` to extract the runtime value of each variable.
  340|       |///  3. Walk `new_expanded` to extract the new literal parts (variable values held fixed).
  341|       |///  4. Rebuild body using original variable references and new literals.
  342|     10|fn attempt_macro_body_fix(

  357|       |
  358|      5|    let mut lits: Vec<&str> = Vec::new();

  361|      5|    for m in var_re.find_iter(body_line) {
                      ^3
  362|      3|        lits.push(&body_line[pos..m.start()]);
  363|      3|        var_refs.push(m.as_str());
  364|      3|        pos = m.end();

  366|      5|    lits.push(&body_line[pos..]);
  367|       |

  370|      3|        if let Some(start) = body_line.find(old_expanded) {
                                  ^0
  371|      0|            let mut s = body_line.to_string();
  372|      0|            s.replace_range(start..start + old_expanded.len(), new_expanded);
  373|      0|            return Some(s);
  374|      3|        }
  375|      3|        return None;
  376|      2|    }
  377|       |
  378|      2|    let mut var_vals: Vec<&str> = Vec::new();
  379|      2|    let mut rem = old_expanded;
  380|      2|    for i in 0..var_refs.len() {

  384|      0|            rem.len()
  385|      2|        } else if next_lit.is_empty() {
  386|      1|            return None; // adjacent variables — ambiguous
  387|       |        } else {
  388|      1|            rem.find(next_lit)?
                                            ^0
  389|       |        };
  390|      1|        var_vals.push(&rem[..end]);
  391|      1|        rem = &rem[end..];
  392|       |    }
  393|      1|    if !rem.starts_with(lits[var_refs.len()]) { return None; }
                                                                     ^0
  394|       |
  395|      1|    let mut new_lits: Vec<String> = Vec::new();

  397|      1|    for var_val in &var_vals {
  398|      1|        let var_pos = new_rem.find(var_val)?;

  399|      1|        new_lits.push(new_rem[..var_pos].to_string());

  401|       |    }

  410|       |

  905|       |/// Try to apply one line replacement to `lines` at `src_line`.

 1748|      1|    fn do_patch_applies_exact_match() {
 1749|      1|        let mut lines = lines("aaa\nbbb\nccc");
 1750|      1|        let mut out = Vec::new();

 1752|      1|        let mut applied = 0;

 1860|       |    // ── attempt_macro_body_fix with vars ────────────────────────────────────
 1861|       |
 1862|       |    #[test]
 1863|      1|    fn attempt_macro_body_fix_with_single_var_updates_literal() {
 1864|       |        // body: "Hello %(name). Bye."
 1865|       |        // old expanded: "Hello Alice. Bye."
 1866|       |        // new expanded: "Hello Alice. Later."
 1867|       |        // Expects the literal suffix " Bye." → " Later." while preserving %(name).
 1868|      1|        let result = attempt_macro_body_fix(
 1869|      1|            "Hello %(name). Bye.",
 1870|      1|            "Hello Alice. Bye.",
 1871|      1|            "Hello Alice. Later.",
 1872|       |            '%',
 1873|       |        );
 1874|      1|        assert!(result.is_some(), "expected Some result, got None");
 1875|      1|        let new_body = result.unwrap();
 1876|      1|        assert!(new_body.contains("Later"), "expected 'Later' in: {new_body}");
 1877|      1|        assert!(new_body.contains("%(name)"), "expected var ref preserved in: {new_body}");
 1878|      1|    }
 1879|       |
 1880|       |    #[test]
 1881|      1|    fn attempt_macro_body_fix_returns_none_when_body_eq_expanded() {
 1882|       |        // body line IS exactly the expanded text → result is just the new expanded text
 1883|      1|        let result = attempt_macro_body_fix("plain text", "plain text", "new text", '%');
 1884|      1|        assert_eq!(result, Some("new text".to_string()));
 1885|      1|    }
 1886|       |    // ── run_apply_back empty database & diff edge cases ─────────────────────
 1887|       |
 1888|       |    struct TestWorkspace {
 1889|       |        root: std::path::PathBuf,
 1890|       |    }
 1891|       |    impl TestWorkspace {
 1892|     19|        fn new() -> Self {
 1893|     19|            let unique = format!(
 1894|       |                "wb-apply-back-tests-{}-{}",
 1895|     19|                std::process::id(),
 1896|     19|                std::time::SystemTime::now().duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH).unwrap().as_nanos()
 1897|       |            );
 1898|     19|            let root = std::env::temp_dir().join(unique);
 1899|     19|            std::fs::create_dir_all(&root).unwrap();
 1900|     19|            Self { root }
 1901|     19|        }
 1902|     15|        fn write_file(&self, rel: &str, content: &[u8]) {
 1903|     15|            let path = self.root.join(rel);
 1904|     15|            if let Some(p) = path.parent() {
 1905|     15|                std::fs::create_dir_all(p).unwrap();
 1906|     15|            }
                          ^0
 1907|     15|            std::fs::write(path, content).unwrap();
 1908|     15|        }
 1909|     18|        fn open_db(&self) -> WeavebackDb {
 1910|     18|            WeavebackDb::open(self.root.join("weaveback.db")).unwrap()
 1911|     18|        }
 1912|       |    }
 1913|       |    impl Drop for TestWorkspace {
 1914|     19|        fn drop(&mut self) {
 1915|     19|            let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&self.root);
 1916|     19|        }
 1917|       |    }
 1918|       |

 1999|      1|        let ws = TestWorkspace::new();
 2000|      1|        let db = ws.open_db();
 2001|      1|        let config = EvalConfig { sigil: '%', ..Default::default() };
 2002|      1|        let resolver = PathResolver::new(ws.root.clone(), ws.root.join("gen"));
 2003|       |
 2004|      1|        let patch_source = resolve_patch_source(
 2005|      1|            "out.rs", 0, 0, &db, &resolver, &config,
 2006|      1|            "src/file.adoc", 10, None, '%', 1
 2007|      1|        ).unwrap();
 2008|       |
 2009|      1|        match patch_source {
 2010|      1|            PatchSource::Noweb { src_file, src_line, len } => {
 2011|      1|                assert_eq!(src_file, "src/file.adoc");
 2012|      1|                assert_eq!(src_line, 10);
 2013|      1|                assert_eq!(len, 1);
 2014|       |            }
 2015|      0|            _ => panic!("Expected Noweb fallback"),
 2016|       |        }
 2017|      1|    }

 2141|      1|            new_text: "    !my_macro(new_val)",

 2145|      1|        };

  651|       |/// Group a `generated_lines` slice into consecutive ranges.
  652|       |/// Returns a JSON array of `{start, end, missed_count}` objects so the
  653|       |/// result can be embedded directly in the summary JSON and consumed by

  677|      2|                }

  679|      1|            }

  682|      5|            "start": ln,

 1516|      0|pub fn run_search(query: String, limit: usize, db_path: PathBuf) -> Result<(), CoverageError> {
 1517|      0|    if !db_path.exists() {
 1518|      0|        return Err(CoverageError::Io(std::io::Error::new(
 1519|      0|            std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound,
 1520|      0|            format!("Database not found at {}. Run weaveback on your source files first.", db_path.display()),
 1521|      0|        )));
 1522|      0|    }
 1523|      0|    let workspace = AgentWorkspace::open(AgentWorkspaceConfig {
 1524|      0|        project_root: std::env::current_dir()?,
 1525|      0|        db_path,
 1526|      0|        gen_dir: PathBuf::from("gen"),
 1527|       |    });
 1528|      0|    let results = workspace.session().search(&query, limit)
 1529|      0|        .map_err(|e| CoverageError::Io(std::io::Error::other(e)))?;
 1530|      0|    if results.is_empty() {
 1531|      0|        println!("No results for {:?}", query);
 1532|      0|        return Ok(());
 1533|      0|    }
 1534|      0|    for r in &results {
 1535|      0|        let channels = if r.channels.is_empty() {
 1536|      0|            String::new()
 1537|       |        } else {
 1538|      0|            format!(" via {}", r.channels.join("+"))
 1539|       |        };
 1540|      0|        if r.tags.is_empty() {
 1541|      0|            println!(
 1542|      0|                "{}:{}-{} [{}]{channels}",
 1543|      0|                r.src_file,
 1544|      0|                r.line_start,
 1545|      0|                r.line_end,
 1546|      0|                r.block_type,
 1547|      0|            );
 1548|      0|        } else {
 1549|      0|            println!(
 1550|      0|                "{}:{}-{} [{}]{channels}  #{}",
 1551|      0|                r.src_file,
 1552|      0|                r.line_start,
 1553|      0|                r.line_end,
 1554|      0|                r.block_type,
 1555|      0|                r.tags.join(","),
 1556|      0|            );
 1557|      0|        }
 1558|      0|        println!("  {}", r.snippet);
 1559|      0|        println!();
 1560|       |    }
 1561|      0|    Ok(())

 1564|      0|pub fn run_tags(file: Option<String>, db_path: PathBuf) -> Result<(), CoverageError> {
 1565|      0|    let blocks = crate::query::list_block_tags(file.as_deref(), &db_path)?;
 1566|      0|    if blocks.is_empty() {
 1567|      0|        println!("No tagged blocks found. Add a [tags] section to weaveback.toml and run wb-tangle.");
 1568|      0|        return Ok(());
 1569|      0|    }
 1570|      0|    let mut current_file = String::new();
 1571|      0|    for b in &blocks {
 1572|      0|        if b.src_file != current_file {
 1573|      0|            println!("\n{}", b.src_file);
 1574|      0|            current_file = b.src_file.clone();
 1575|      0|        }
 1576|      0|        println!("  :{} [{}]  #{}", b.line_start, b.block_type, b.tags);
 1577|       |    }

 1579|      0|    Ok(())

 1582|      0|pub fn run_trace(
 1583|      0|    out_file: String,
 1584|      0|    line: u32,
 1585|      0|    col: u32,
 1586|      0|    db_path: PathBuf,
 1587|      0|    gen_dir: PathBuf,
 1588|      0|    eval_config: weaveback_macro::evaluator::EvalConfig
 1589|      0|) -> Result<(), CoverageError> {
 1590|      0|    let db = open_db(&db_path)?;
 1591|      0|    let project_root = std::env::current_dir().unwrap_or_default();
 1592|      0|    let resolver = PathResolver::new(project_root, gen_dir);
 1593|       |
 1594|      0|    match lookup::perform_trace(&out_file, line, col, &db, &resolver, eval_config) {
 1595|      0|        Ok(Some(json)) => {
 1596|      0|            println!("{}", serde_json::to_string_pretty(&json).unwrap());
 1597|      0|            Ok(())
 1598|       |        }
 1599|       |        Ok(None) => {
 1600|      0|            eprintln!("No mapping found for {}:{}", out_file, line);
 1601|      0|            Ok(())
 1602|       |        }
 1603|      0|        Err(lookup::LookupError::InvalidInput(msg)) => {
 1604|      0|            Err(CoverageError::Io(std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::InvalidInput, msg)))
 1605|       |        }
 1606|      0|        Err(lookup::LookupError::Db(e)) => Err(CoverageError::Noweb(WeavebackError::Db(e))),
 1607|      0|        Err(lookup::LookupError::Io(e)) => Err(CoverageError::Io(e)),
 1608|       |    }

 2435|      1|    fn test_parse_lcov_records_simple() {
 2436|      1|        let lcov = "SF:file.rs\nDA:1,10\nDA:2,0\nend_of_record\nSF:other.rs\nDA:5,1\nend_of_record\n";
 2437|      1|        let records = parse_lcov_records(lcov);

 2444|       |    #[test]
 2445|      1|    fn test_compute_unmapped_ranges() {
 2446|      1|        let lines = vec![
 2447|      1|            json!({"generated_line": 1, "hit_count": 5}),
 2448|      1|            json!({"generated_line": 2, "hit_count": 0}),
 2449|      1|            json!({"generated_line": 3, "hit_count": 0}),
 2450|      1|            json!({"generated_line": 5, "hit_count": 1}),

  781|     23|fn send_response<W: Write>(writer: &mut W, id: Option<Value>, result: Value) {
  782|     23|    let mut resp = json!({ "jsonrpc": "2.0" });
  783|     23|    if let Some(id) = id {
  784|     23|        resp.as_object_mut().unwrap().insert("id".to_string(), id);
  785|     23|        resp.as_object_mut().unwrap().insert("result".to_string(), result);
  786|     23|    }
                  ^0
  787|     23|    let _ = writeln!(writer, "{}", serde_json::to_string(&resp).unwrap());
  788|     23|}

  790|      8|fn send_text<W: Write>(writer: &mut W, id: Option<Value>, text: &str) {

  793|       |    }));

  796|     12|fn send_error<W: Write>(writer: &mut W, id: Option<Value>, msg: &str) {

  850|      1|        let input = r#"{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":100,"method":"initialize"}
  851|      1|{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":101,"method":"tools/list"}
  852|      1|"#;

  854|      1|        let mut writer = Vec::new();
  855|      1|        let db_path = PathBuf::from("nonexistent.db");
  856|      1|        let gen_dir = PathBuf::from("gen");
  857|      1|        let eval_config = EvalConfig::default();
  858|       |
  859|      1|        let project_root = std::env::current_dir().unwrap();
  860|      1|        let result = run_mcp(reader, &mut writer, db_path, gen_dir, project_root, eval_config);
  861|      1|        assert!(result.is_ok());
  862|       |

  864|      1|        assert!(output.contains("\"id\":100"));
  865|      1|        assert!(output.contains("\"protocolVersion\":\"2024-11-05\""));

  870|       |    // ── Test helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  871|       |
  872|       |    struct McpWorkspace {
  873|       |        root: std::path::PathBuf,
  874|       |    }
  875|       |    impl McpWorkspace {
  876|     23|        fn new() -> Self {
  877|     23|            let id = format!(
  878|       |                "wb-mcp-tests-{}-{}",
  879|     23|                std::process::id(),
  880|     23|                std::time::SystemTime::now()
  881|     23|                    .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
  882|     23|                    .unwrap()
  883|     23|                    .as_nanos()
  884|       |            );
  885|     23|            let root = std::env::temp_dir().join(id);
  886|     23|            std::fs::create_dir_all(&root).unwrap();
  887|     23|            let root = root.canonicalize().unwrap();
  888|     23|            Self { root }
  889|     23|        }
  890|     30|        fn db_path(&self) -> PathBuf { self.root.join("weaveback.db") }
  891|     25|        fn gen_dir(&self) -> PathBuf { self.root.join("gen") }
  892|      4|        fn open_db(&self) -> WeavebackDb { WeavebackDb::open(self.db_path()).unwrap() }
  893|      3|        fn write_file(&self, rel_path: &str, content: &[u8]) {
  894|      3|            let p = self.root.join(rel_path);
  895|      3|            if let Some(parent) = p.parent() {
  896|      3|                std::fs::create_dir_all(parent).unwrap();
  897|      3|            }
                          ^0
  898|      3|            std::fs::write(p, content).unwrap();
  899|      3|        }
  900|       |    }
  901|       |    impl Drop for McpWorkspace {
  902|     23|        fn drop(&mut self) { let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&self.root); }
  903|       |    }
  904|       |
  905|     23|    fn mcp_drive(ws: &McpWorkspace, requests: &str) -> String {
  906|     23|        let reader = std::io::Cursor::new(requests.to_string());
  907|     23|        let mut writer = Vec::new();
  908|     23|        run_mcp(reader, &mut writer, ws.db_path(), ws.gen_dir(), ws.root.clone(), EvalConfig::default()).unwrap();
  909|     23|        String::from_utf8(writer).unwrap()
  910|     23|    }
  911|       |

  649|       |    #[test]
  650|      1|    fn compute_skip_set_propagates_dirty_chunks() {
  651|      1|        let tmp = tempdir().unwrap();
  652|      1|        let db_path = tmp.path().join("prev.db");
  653|       |
  654|      1|        let mut prev_db = WeavebackDb::open(&db_path).unwrap();
  655|       |        // Chunk B depends on Chunk A
  656|      1|        prev_db.set_chunk_defs(&[
  657|      1|            weaveback_tangle::db::ChunkDefEntry {
  658|      1|                src_file: "src.adoc".into(),
  659|      1|                chunk_name: "A".into(),
  660|      1|                nth: 0,
  661|      1|                def_start: 1,
  662|      1|                def_end: 10,
  663|      1|            },
  664|      1|            weaveback_tangle::db::ChunkDefEntry {
  665|      1|                src_file: "src.adoc".into(),
  666|      1|                chunk_name: "B".into(),
  667|      1|                nth: 0,
  668|      1|                def_start: 11,
  669|      1|                def_end: 20,
  670|      1|            },
  671|      1|        ]).unwrap();
  672|      1|        prev_db.set_chunk_deps(&[("B".into(), "A".into(), "src.adoc".into())]).unwrap();
  673|       |
  674|       |        // Block 0 covers lines 1-10 (Chunk A)
  675|      1|        let block_a = weaveback_tangle::block_parser::SourceBlockEntry {
  676|      1|            block_index: 0,
  677|      1|            block_type: "code".into(),
  678|      1|            line_start: 1,
  679|      1|            line_end: 10,
  680|      1|            content_hash: [0u8; 32],
  681|      1|        };
  682|      1|        prev_db.set_source_blocks("src.adoc", &[block_a.clone()]).unwrap();
  683|       |
  684|      1|        let mut current_db = WeavebackDb::open_temp().unwrap();
  685|      1|        let mut source_contents = HashMap::new();
  686|       |        // Use content that will trigger the same block index but different hash
  687|       |        // We'll mock the blocks directly because compute_skip_set calls parse_source_blocks
  688|       |        // which we can't easily mock across crates without real content.
  689|      1|        source_contents.insert("src.adoc".to_string(), "<<A>>=\nnew content\n@".to_string());
  690|       |
  691|      1|        let skip = compute_skip_set(&source_contents, &Some(prev_db), &mut current_db, tmp.path());

    2|       |//!
    3|       |//! Runs as an optional post-step after `wb-tangle`.  Only blocks
    4|       |//! whose BLAKE3 content hash has changed since the last run are sent to

  147|      2|fn build_prompt(items: &[(usize, &str, &str)]) -> String {
  148|       |    // items: (local_index, block_type, first_line_of_content)

  162|      5|fn parse_response(response: &str) -> Vec<(usize, String)> {
  163|      5|    response
  164|      5|        .lines()
  165|      9|        .filter_map(|line| {
                       ^5
  166|      9|            let (idx_str, tags_str) = line.split_once(':')?;
                                                                        ^0
  167|      9|            let idx: usize = idx_str.trim().parse().ok()?;
                              ^8   ^8                                 ^1
  168|      8|            let tags: Vec<&str> = tags_str
  169|      8|                .split(',')
  170|      8|                .map(str::trim)
  171|     11|                .filter(|t| !t.is_empty())
                               ^8
  172|      8|                .collect();
  173|      8|            if tags.is_empty() {
  174|      1|                return None;
  175|      7|            }
  176|       |            // Sanitise: lowercase, keep alphanumeric and hyphens only.
  177|      7|            let clean: String = tags
  178|      7|                .iter()

  180|     10|                    t.to_lowercase()

  186|      7|                .collect::<Vec<_>>()
  187|      7|                .join(",");
  188|      7|            if clean.is_empty() { None } else { Some((idx, clean)) }
                                                ^1            ^6
  189|      9|        })
  190|      5|        .collect()

  193|       |/// Return the first non-empty line of a block given 1-based line numbers.
  194|       |/// `line_start` and `line_end` are 1-based; returns `""` when out of range.
  195|      3|fn block_first_line(source: &str, line_start: u32, line_end: u32) -> String {
  196|      3|    let lo = (line_start as usize).saturating_sub(1);
  197|      3|    let hi = (line_end as usize).min(source.lines().count());
  198|      3|    source
  199|      3|        .lines()
  200|      3|        .skip(lo)
  201|      3|        .take(hi.saturating_sub(lo))
  202|      3|        .next()
  203|      3|        .unwrap_or("")
  204|      3|        .to_string()

  206|       |/// Tag all prose blocks that have no cached tag or whose content changed.
  207|       |/// Silently skips on API errors (just warns to stderr).
  208|      5|pub fn run_auto_tag(db: &mut WeavebackDb, cfg: &TagConfig) {
  209|      5|    let blocks = match db.get_blocks_needing_tags() {
  210|      5|        Ok(b) => b,
  211|      0|        Err(e) => { eprintln!("warning: auto-tag db query failed: {e}"); return; }
  212|       |    };
  213|      5|    if blocks.is_empty() { return; }
                                         ^3      ^2
  214|       |
  215|       |    // Group blocks by file so we only fetch each snapshot once.
  216|      2|    let mut by_file: std::collections::HashMap<String, Vec<_>> =
  217|      2|        std::collections::HashMap::new();
  218|      2|    for b in blocks {
  219|      2|        by_file.entry(b.src_file.clone()).or_default().push(b);
  220|      2|    }
  221|       |
  222|      2|    let batch_size = cfg.batch_size.max(1);
  223|      2|    let mut tagged = 0usize;
  224|       |
  225|      2|    for (src_file, file_blocks) in &by_file {
  226|       |        // Fetch snapshot; skip file if not found.
  227|      2|        let snapshot = match db.get_src_snapshot(src_file) {
                          ^1
  228|      1|            Ok(Some(bytes)) => match String::from_utf8(bytes) {
  229|      1|                Ok(s) => s,
  230|      0|                Err(_) => continue,
  231|       |            },
  232|       |            _ => {
  233|       |                // Try normalised path variants.
  234|      1|                let alt = src_file.strip_prefix("./").unwrap_or(src_file);
  235|      1|                match db.get_src_snapshot(alt) {
  236|      0|                    Ok(Some(bytes)) => String::from_utf8(bytes).unwrap_or_default(),
  237|      1|                    _ => continue,
  238|       |                }
  239|       |            }
  240|       |        };
  241|       |
  242|      1|        for chunk in file_blocks.chunks(batch_size) {
  243|       |            // Build (local_index, block_type, first_line) tuples for the prompt.
  244|      1|            let items: Vec<(usize, &str, String)> = chunk
  245|      1|                .iter()
  246|      1|                .enumerate()
  247|      1|                .map(|(i, b)| {
  248|      1|                    let first = block_first_line(&snapshot, b.line_start, b.line_end);
  249|      1|                    (i, b.block_type.as_str(), first)
  250|      1|                })
  251|      1|                .collect();
  252|       |
  253|      1|            let prompt_items: Vec<(usize, &str, &str)> = items
  254|      1|                .iter()
  255|      1|                .map(|(i, bt, fl)| (*i, *bt, fl.as_str()))
  256|      1|                .collect();
  257|       |
  258|      1|            let response = match call_llm(cfg, &build_prompt(&prompt_items)) {
                              ^0
  259|      0|                Ok(r) => r,
  260|      1|                Err(e) => {
  261|      1|                    eprintln!("warning: auto-tag LLM call failed: {e}");
  262|      1|                    continue;
  263|       |                }
  264|       |            };
  265|       |
  266|       |            // Accumulate results before writing to avoid partial commits on error.
  267|      0|            let results = parse_response(&response);
  268|      0|            for (local_idx, tags) in results {
  269|      0|                if let Some(b) = chunk.get(local_idx) {
  270|      0|                    if let Err(e) = db.set_block_tags(
  271|      0|                        &b.src_file,
  272|      0|                        b.block_index,
  273|      0|                        &b.content_hash,
  274|      0|                        &tags,
  275|      0|                    ) {
  276|      0|                        eprintln!("warning: auto-tag store failed: {e}");
  277|      0|                    } else {
  278|      0|                        tagged += 1;
  279|      0|                    }
  280|      0|                }
  281|       |            }
  282|       |        }
  283|       |    }
  284|       |
  285|      2|    if tagged > 0 {
  286|      0|        eprintln!("auto-tag: tagged {tagged} block(s)");
  287|      2|    }

   99|       |/// Run every pass in `weaveback.toml` and, if a db exists, rebuild FTS /
  100|       |/// run LLM tagging / run embedding.
  101|       |///
  102|       |/// Returns `Err` if config cannot be read/parsed or if any pass fails.
  103|      3|pub fn run_tangle_all(
  104|      3|    config_path: &std::path::Path,
  105|      3|    force_generated: bool,
  106|      3|) -> Result<(), std::io::Error> {
  107|      3|    let src = std::fs::read_to_string(config_path)
                      ^2
  108|      3|        .map_err(|e| std::io::Error::new(e.kind(),
                                   ^1                  ^1^1
  109|      1|            format!("{}: {e}", config_path.display())))?;
  110|      2|    let cfg: TangleCfg = toml::from_str(&src)
                      ^1   ^1
  111|      2|        .map_err(|e| std::io::Error::other(
                                   ^1
  112|      1|            format!("{}: {e}", config_path.display())))?;
  113|       |
  114|      1|    let exe = std::env::current_exe()?;
                                                   ^0
  115|      1|    let default_gen = cfg.default_gen.as_deref().unwrap_or(".");
  116|       |
  117|      1|    for pass in &cfg.passes {
  118|      1|        let mut cmd = build_pass_cmd(&exe, pass, default_gen, force_generated);
  119|      1|        match cmd.status() {
  120|      0|            Err(e) => {
  121|      0|                return Err(std::io::Error::other(format!("{}: {e}", pass.dir)));
  122|       |            }
  123|      1|            Ok(s) if !s.success() => {
  124|      1|                return Err(std::io::Error::other(format!(
  125|      1|                    "tangle pass failed for: {}",
  126|      1|                    pass.dir
  127|      1|                )));
  128|       |            }
  129|      0|            Ok(_) => {}
  130|       |        }
  131|       |    }
  132|       |
  133|      0|    let db_path = std::path::Path::new("weaveback.db");
  134|      0|    if db_path.exists() {
  135|      0|        match weaveback_tangle::db::WeavebackDb::open(db_path) {
  136|      0|            Ok(mut db) => {
  137|      0|                if let Some(tags_cfg) = &cfg.tags {
  138|      0|                    crate::tag::run_auto_tag(&mut db, &crate::tag::TagConfig {
  139|      0|                        backend:    tags_cfg.backend.clone(),
  140|      0|                        model:      tags_cfg.model.clone(),
  141|      0|                        endpoint:   tags_cfg.endpoint.clone(),
  142|      0|                        batch_size: tags_cfg.batch_size,
  143|      0|                    });
  144|      0|                }
  145|      0|                if let Some(embed_cfg) = &cfg.embeddings {
  146|      0|                    crate::semantic::run_auto_embed(&mut db, &crate::semantic::EmbeddingConfig {
  147|      0|                        backend:    embed_cfg.backend.clone(),
  148|      0|                        model:      embed_cfg.model.clone(),
  149|      0|                        endpoint:   embed_cfg.endpoint.clone(),
  150|      0|                        batch_size: embed_cfg.batch_size,
  151|      0|                    });
  152|      0|                }
  153|      0|                if let Err(e) = db.rebuild_prose_fts(None) {
  154|      0|                    eprintln!("warning: FTS index rebuild failed: {e}");
  155|      0|                }
  156|       |            }
  157|      0|            Err(e) => eprintln!("warning: could not open db for FTS rebuild: {e}"),
  158|       |        }
  159|      0|    }
